haññadatthatthipasaṃsalābhā

sandhi. there is (no) benefit other than gaining praise; there is (no) purpose other than praise and gain; lit. certainly other benefit-there is praise gain [hi + añña + attha + atthi + pasaṃsā + lābhā] ✓

Grammar sandhi, ind + adj + masc + pr + fem + masc
Meaning there is (no) benefit other than gaining praise; there is (no) purpose other than praise and gain; lit. certainly other benefit-there is praise gain
Construction hi + añña + attha + atthi + pasaṃsā + lābhā
Commentary (SNPa) na h'añña'd'atth'atthi pasaṃsalābhā'ti na hi ettha pasaṃsalābhato añño attho atthi.
Sanskrit hi + anya + artha + asti + praśaṃsā + lābha

Example

etesu ugghāti nighāti hoti,
etam'pi disvā virame kath'ojjaṃ,
na h'añña'd'atth'atthipasaṃsalābhā.

Notes see hatāvakāsa 2
Sanskrit hata + avakāśa

Example

assaddho akataññū ca,
sandhicchedo ca yo naro,
hat'āvakāso vant'āso,
sa ve uttamaporiso.

Sanskrit hrīvera

Example

Commentary (SNa) hīn'attarūpā na pāraṃ gamā te'ti hīn'attasabhāvā te nibbānaṅgamā na honti. hīn'attharūpā'ti'pi pāṭho, hīn'atthajātikā parihīn'atthā'ti attho. (SNt) hīn'attarūpā'ti hīn'ādhimuttikatāya nihīnacittasabhāvā.
Sanskrit hīnārtha + rūpa

Example

tapassī brāhmaṇā caraṃ,
cittañ'ca nesaṃ na sammā vimuttaṃ,
hīn'attharūpā na pāraṅ'gamā te.

Commentary (VINa) yasmā pana gihī vā upāsako vā ārāmiko vā sāmaṇero vā hutvā dānasaraṇasīlasaṃvar'ādīhi saggamaggaṃ vā jhānavimokkh'ādīhi mokkhamaggaṃ vā ārādhetuṃ bhabbo hoti, tasm'āssa gihi'ādibhāvo visuddhi nāma hoti, tasmā taṃ visuddhiṃ apekkhanato, visuddh'āpekkho'ti vuccati. ten'eva c'assa padabhājane, gihī vā hotu'kāmo'tiādi vuttaṃ.
Sanskrit bhavitum + kāma

Example

visuddh'āpekkho'ti gihī vā hotu'kāmo upāsako vā hotu'kāmo ārāmiko vā hotu'kāmo sāmaṇero vā hotu'kāmo.

VIN 1.1.4 catutthapārājikaṃ
hotuṃ

inf. (+acc) to be; to become [√hū + a + tuṃ] ✓

Grammar inf of hoti, trans (+acc)
Meaning to be; to become
Root Family √hū
Root √hū･1 a (be)
Base √hū + a > ho
Construction ho + tuṃ
Phonetic Change ū > o
Synonym bhavituṃ
Sanskrit bhavitum
Sanskrit Root √bhū 1 (be)

Example

so lābhasakkāraṃ jigucchanto pabbajjaṃ anupagantvā, pahomi c'āhaṃ lābh'ālābh'ādīsu nibbikāro hotun'ti attānaṃ takkento, visesato paraparibhavasahanādipaṭipadaṃ pūrento upekkhāpāramiṃ matthakaṃ pāpessāmī'ti

CPa 3.15 mahālomahaṃsacariyāvaṇṇanā
hoteva

sandhi. there is just; there exists some [hoti + eva] ✓

Grammar sandhi, pr + ind
Meaning there is just; there exists some
Construction hoti + eva
Commentary (ANa) hot'eva kaṅkhā'ti hoti'y'eva kaṅkhā
Sanskrit bhavati + eva

Example

tesaṃ no, bhante, amhākaṃ hot'eva kaṅkhā hoti vicikicchā, ko su nāma imesaṃ bhavataṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ saccaṃ āha, ko musā'ti? alañ'hi vo, kālāmā, kaṅkhituṃ alaṃ vicikicchituṃ. kaṅkhanīy'eva pana vo ṭhāne vicikicchā uppannā.
